<Resp>None<//Resp><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPql5MxQxmzWjbez8YpXDyjM11aOwFaOpF_dJRl=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNqB1lnrJFIMwZVIOdDy8sx_vlmoO8ixniXZRrK=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNXDq95O4iZOv92qNm-MyefocDlts1yy4zuGdXY=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pics><Review>As i stated last week, we had a piece of cake that was too cold to evaluate so i postponed writing about the MB's bakery goods until today.
So i went in fully thinking that i would order a piece of cake and hightail it out. But all of the different aromas emanating from the back of the house pretty much made me order several things.
Martin is once again at the front desk being his charming self and unconsciously coerced me into ordering:
Chicken Tinga Tacos
Hibiscus Tea
Carrot Cake Muffin and
Slice of Coconut Layer Cake which i eventually brought home
First things first: the the Coconut Cake:
The cake itself is crumbly and coco-nutty obviously flavored with natural coconut flavor as in coconut milk. This cake is a coconut lovers delight!
It is nicely rested and room temp when i eat it and as such all of the sugars, flavors and fats are settled and ready for my devouring.  And devour i did. God help me. (obviously today was Carb day!)
The frosting is light and the buttercream is flavored with coconut water? coconut milk? Whatever: it is delicious. Also: the top of the cake is soaked with coco-sugar syrup just to amplify the coconut flavor.
Cakes need to be eaten at room temp. The only cakes i eat refrigerated are those with mousse or whipped cream. This Coconut Cake is Very Good Stuff!
Carrot Cake Muffin:
the muffins are served room temp and therefore ready to glom immediately. this product is chock full of raisins, carrots and walnuts and is BIG!: as in a muffin on steroids. All of the flavors are clean and upfront: the muffin texture itself crumbly and moist. ( aren't muffins a thing so that we can eat cake for breakfast?)
And i do not miss it not having frosting at all.
Chicken Tinga Tacos:
The best thing about the tacos is that they are made on house produced corn tortillas. The torts are redolent of corn masa, the chicken is citrusy and slightly spicy from Chipotle and the red onions are crispy yet spicy. Good not Great.
You can buy whole 8", 3 layer cakes for 45 bucks which to me is the norm and below for a cake of this high quality and worth every penny.
Love this place.</Review></record>

Could be improved... pricing is not transparent. Prices have been inflated recently (went in for a $19 cleanup--salon territory). As for customer experience, it feels like an assembly line--in and out.

The small and cramped space can be a problem for kids or a group. It does get noisy with people talking over you due to the tight space. That may be a problem to some. They specialize in classic cuts so take that into consideration if you are looking for modern/trendy cuts. Not a lot of customer personalization.

As for my experience, great haircut but not what I expected. Would have liked for the barber to take personal styling and grooming into consideration. Hair grows back so no major complaints.<//Text>

< review>
El Comal Family Restaurant is located in an old looking shopping center, the parking is terrible, and traffic in and out is atrocious.  However, once you open the door you enter a colorful tropical atmosphere, adorned with classic Hispanic artwork throughout. The food was good. I had the Caldo de Pollo (chicken soup) which was very good. The broth was light and well flavored, vegetables were cooked just right, and I was given a large piece of chicken (on the bone). The taste brought instant gratification, as it reminded me of the soup my grandmother would make when I was a child. We got a lot of food (see picture) for a great price. Everything pictured including drinks was just $27! If you are in the area, and not in a hurry, stop by and enjoy a bite to eat.<//review>

<user_name>JESSICA< /user_name><date>1574544351632< /date><Rating>5<//Rating><text>El Comal Family Restaurant is located in an old looking shopping center, the parking is terrible, and traffic in and out is atrocious.  However, once you open the door you enter a colorful tropical atmosphere, adorned with classic Hispanic artwork throughout. The food was good. I had the Caldo de Pollo (chicken soup) which was very good. The broth was light and well flavored, vegetables were cooked just right, and I was given a large piece of chicken (on the bone). The taste brought instant gratification, as it reminded me of the soup my grandmother would make when I was a child. We got a lot of food (see picture) for a great price. Everything pictured including drinks was just $27! If you are in the area, and not in a hurry, stop by and enjoy a bite to eat.<//text><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO9Dp5uq2pwGxue3OoscrMZqE87zG3U8h-Uasec=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN4iInxiJJ00j51azBPD67IRzBwPHLUhdIbscoR=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNMAqeRV6rPnfok4htRBVKusB6u7PnPLGIZWltD=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipModSJywK1TBfWFcsil_2c70DDpn0BCBZQKIWdA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pictures>< Resp>

<Text>My dad and mom were patrons of El Comal since the old location.  With mom gone now dad insists on his visits.  Hesitantly I always abided.  Customer Service is key for me.  Food is second.  Lets start with service.   And I understand not everyone is meant for the industry, but for the most part this staff is fine.  With the exception of one.  TAKE NOTE;  Ysenia far exceeds any exceptions one would find at a restaurant.  You typically find her level of service in fine dining.  i would definitely keep my eye on her and write my SOP (standard operating procedure) for all new hires that are going to be working the floor.

Now the food, as my dad is a fan, i became one too with reservation.  The food is good, all the dishes I've tried so far had been done well.  The pupusas are amazing if you eat there.  Don't take home.    Their Chile  Verde was also great.  Now thier hard shell shredded beef tacos are KILLER.  Why am i not raving about their food.  Well I am.  As i would of any other latin restaurant that served food my grandmother could easily out perform.  I am hispanic and know latin food.  I say this with love and in hopes my comments assist.  I could get this at most good mexican restaurants.  But who want good.  I want GREAT!  A little kick in authenticity would go a long way.  A pinch in presentation i believe essential.  I begin eating with my eyes before it touches my mouth.

We will be back, my father insists.  I love the new decor.  The bar looks amazing and $15 FOR BOTTOMLESS MIMOSA BRUCH!  Im there!!!  IF MY FATHER BELIEVES IN YOU IM SURE I WILL TOO!!!!!<//Text>< pictures>

< Review>
El Comal is without a doubt this region's best choice for authentic Mexican style food. Place is beautiful. Should be a historical town landmark now that El Comal is occupying the spot. These guys were a hit decades before moving to this location. I'll eat at El Comal before I go to any of the other like cuisines here. I'm just happy they re-opened after their fire. Anyways take this advice... nowhere can you go in this town to find a better experience. They have a private party room for b-days, weddings, cinses, whatever. They have a bar with game television coverages that you can dine at as well as regular booth and table seating. Uber family friendly oriented. The decor is really cool. When the El Comal family had to move from their last place they used their insurance re-build money wisely. Their new location is bomb. Food is (as usual) bomb, people are no, not bomb... loveable and special. Good family operation. The Dogman of Lake Elsinore has spoken...so be it...and they all said...Amen!<//Review>

El Comal is without a doubt this region's best choice for authentic Mexican style food. Place is beautiful. Should be a historical town landmark now that El Comal is occupying the spot. These guys were a hit decades before moving to this location. I'll eat at El Comal before I go to any of the other like cuisines here. I'm just happy they re-opened after their fire. Anyways take this advice... nowhere can you go in this town to find a better experience. They have a private party room for b-days, weddings, cinses, whatever. They have a bar with game television coverages that you can dine at as well as regular booth and table seating. Uber family friendly oriented. The decor is really cool. When the El Comal family had to move from their last place they used their insurance re-build money wisely. Their new location is bomb. Food is (as usual) bomb, people are no, not bomb... loveable and special. Good family operation. The Dogman of Lake Elsinore has spoken...so be it...and they all said...Amen!< /review>
